Current Commentary

Anti-Japanese Resistance and Port Blockade

As the Japanese Empire contemplates withdrawing from the League of Nations, it suddenly issued an opinion on the so-called blockade issue in the form of a statement by a responsible person. The statement said that countries around the world will not blockade Japan because Japan withdraws from the League of Nations. If Japan is indeed subjected to a blockade, the Japanese navy can immediately blockade Chinese ports, cutting off all countries' trade with China. At the same time, Japan can enforce trade to maintain its economy during extraordinary times. We have repeatedly stated the incompetence of the League of Nations. We have also determined that its so-called economic sanctions are merely a tool for deceiving people because the great powers will never sacrifice their trade with Japan for the sake of the China issue. Therefore, the statement that "countries around the world will not blockade Japan because Japan withdraws from the League of Nations" can be said to have a clear understanding of the weaknesses of the League of Nations. Looking back at those in our country who advocate compromise, they are still seeking a diplomatic solution in a way that is akin to consulting deities and divination. It can be said that they are foolish and ignorant.

Secondly, if the Japanese navy wants to blockade our country's ports, it would be a very easy task, except for Guangdong and Guangxi. Since Ryukyu and Taiwan have fallen into enemy hands, the Japanese Empire has geographically created a semi-circular encirclement line around China. If the people of the country have time to look at a map of Asia, they will know that the statement is not false. Under this kind of natural situation, the Japanese only need to use the activity of submarines to fully implement an effective encirclement. This encirclement starts from Hebei and Shandong in the north and extends to Fujian and Zhejiang in the south. Only the Pearl River basin, due to the presence of British forces, may be able to find shelter and be spared. For more than twenty years, ignorant military men in our country have been indulging in internal warfare. The so-called national defense has long been forgotten. Once a sudden incident occurs, they realize that they have become turtles in a jar. Who is responsible for this? How can we not be heartbroken?

Thirdly, the so-called forced trade has already begun during the January 28th Incident. The areas around Tianjin, Jinan, and Jiaozhou have even become accustomed to it. At that time, the weak local officials, intimidated by the threat of Japanese gunboats, voluntarily prohibited the people from opposing Japan. Unscrupulous merchants even used the meager profits from Japanese goods to exploit the people's hard-earned money. The gains from trade within the country were used to complete the needs of aggression within the country. This was already a fact. Therefore, the so-called maintenance of the economy during extraordinary times has long been in its embryonic form. It would be a big mistake to think of forced trade as forced buying and selling.

From the above, it is obvious that China's resistance against Japan must be an anti-imperialist national revolution. If China cannot abandon the ports, which are in fact the main base for imperialist economic aggression, with the courage of a warrior cutting off his wrist, and sacrifice the immature national capital controlled by imperialist capital forces, then it will definitely not dare to talk about war. And at this time when the lifeline of finance is tied to trade and the concentration of financial power in the ports, it is impossible to talk about war without preparing for a drastic reform of financial policy and the monetary system. Only with such determination and such perseverance can we automatically impose a counter-blockade on the ports, so that the vast inland areas will no longer be the consumer market for the various treaty ports under imperialist forces. Only then can we break the Japanese evil scheme of using Chinese to control Chinese. Only then can we make the conflicts of interest between the great powers intensify rapidly due to the blockage of the Chinese market. However, how can this be hoped for from those in the country who are content with the status quo, indulge in pleasure, and refuse to repent?

Germany Does Not Forget Former Overseas Territories

Japan Does Not Abandon Mandated Islands

Causes Extreme Concern in the German Government

(Berlin) The issue of returning Germany's overseas territories has now become an important part of Germany's foreign policy. The National Socialist government attaches great importance to Japan's declaration that even if Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, it cannot return the Pacific islands that were previously entrusted to it for administration. Today, official sources said that this issue can only be resolved by the League of Nations Council and the Mandates Commission. If the League of Nations Council and the Mandates Commission can handle this matter, the German government will take a stand to protect all the interests of Germany's territories. (Reuters, 22nd)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Foreign Ministry received a report from its embassy in Germany stating that the German government issued a statement yesterday saying that the issue of the mandate over the South Pacific Islands must be resolved by the League of Nations Council and the Mandates Commission. The German government has decided to assert its demands in these two bodies and will not express anything separately to Japan. Although the Japanese government has withdrawn from the League of Nations, the Mandates Commission has decided to participate. Therefore, after withdrawing from the League of Nations, it will have a more serious conflict with the countries of the League of Nations. The Japanese Foreign Ministry considers this statement an important issue and will carefully study how to deal with it. (China United Press, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The German government has officially declared its attitude on the issue of the South Pacific Mandate. The Japanese naval authorities are very nervous about this. They are awaiting a public announcement from the Japanese military attaché in Germany. The South Pacific Mandate is Japan's maritime lifeline. The "Withdrawal from the League of Nations and the South Pacific Mandate" issued by the Naval Military Education Department today contains the following views: (1) The South Pacific Islands were occupied by the Japanese Navy after participating in World War I. During World War I, it was agreed between Japan and the United Kingdom that Japan would acquire the territories after the end of World War I. (2) However, as a result of participating in the war, the United States obtained the right to speak at the peace conference and opposed the annexation of Germany's colonies. Therefore, the four countries of Britain, France, Italy, and Japan abandoned the name and took the reality, assigning the territories to Japan under the name of administering them on behalf of the League of Nations. (3) However, this assignment was decided before the establishment of the League of Nations, and the South Pacific Islands were not mandated by the League of Nations. Therefore, the League of Nations has no right to change the mandatory power. (4) In short, the so-called League of Nations mandate means that sovereignty does not lie with the League of Nations but with Japan. Therefore, even if it withdraws, there is no need to give up. (Dentsu, 23rd)

(Geneva) It is expected that if Japan formally notifies its withdrawal from the League of Nations and still declares its desire to retain the mandated islands in the Pacific, the Allied Powers may convene a meeting to discuss the matter. Recent statements by Japan and Germany on the issue of the disposition of these islands have caused great concern here. It is expected that this will become a thorny crisis. Furthermore, it is heard that Washington has already notified the League of Nations that if Japan attempts to retain the islands after leaving the League of Nations, the United States will be extremely concerned. Legal experts agree that the former German colonies nominally still belong to the Allied Powers, and the League of Nations is only acting as a custodian. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

(Geneva) Japan's desire to continue to hold the governing islands in the Pacific after its withdrawal from the League of Nations has now become a major topic of discussion at the League of Nations. These islands belonged to Germany before the European War. Therefore, both the League of Nations and Germany feel a very keen interest in this issue, and they both feel that this matter cannot be resolved solely by Japan. It must be handled jointly by various countries through international treaties. The principles of the League of Nations' governing methods will inevitably be affected as a result. Therefore, Germany will also be able to have the opportunity to state its views when this issue is brought up for discussion in the future. (National Telegraph, 22nd)

(Berlin) Today, reliable sources here reported that after Japan formally notifies its withdrawal from the League of Nations, the German government will request the return of the Pacific islands administered by Japan when the League of Nations Mandates Commission meets to discuss the issue. However, according to sources close to the Hitler government, Germany does not want to beg for help from the League of Nations. It would rather the League of Nations launch it on its own. At present, the whole of Germany is paying very close attention to the fate of these islands. Today's Kolnische Zeitung editorial stated that the Japanese government's declaration that it still wants to retain the Pacific mandated islands has raised an extremely serious issue. This matter concerns principles, so it is of great importance to Germany. This is a basic issue concerning the mandate system and falls within the jurisdiction of the League of Nations. It cannot be considered solely from Japan's perspective. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

Saito Determined to Find an Opportunity to Step Down

Cabinet Change Within Seven Months

Urging Finance Minister to Maintain the Status Quo

Various Political Parties Actively Mobilizing

National League Advocates Hiranuma Cabinet

Minzheng Party Supports Ugaki Kazushige

Kinno-to Demands Imperial Relative to Take Power

(Tokyo) With only two days left before the close of the Japanese Diet, political circles are focusing on the issue of the successor cabinet. Prime Minister Saito met with Home Minister Yamamoto again in the Diet this morning at 11:00 AM, and they reached a consensus on the issue of stepping down. They are only waiting for an opportunity to step down after the end of the Diet. As for the issue of the successor cabinet, the claims of the various factions are unusually divergent. The Seiyukai advocates that President Suzuki should form a strong party cabinet and may cooperate with friendly parties. The Minzheng Party advocates that Saito should reorganize the cabinet and continue to rule, otherwise hand it over to Korean Governor Ugaki to organize a military cabinet based on the Minzheng Party. The National League advocates the establishment of the Hiranuma Cabinet and close cooperation with the military. What is most noteworthy is the fascist party's advocacy of an imperial relative cabinet, implementing a "Kinno-to Revolution" and using the authority of the imperial family to silence the opposition. All opponents will be charged with treason. They plan to eliminate dissenters. According to Kinno-to, in October 1931, after the September 18th Incident, they supported a certain imperial relative to carry out the Kinno-to Revolution, but failed in advance. This time, they are taking the opportunity to be active again, using young military men as a background. On the surface, it is presided over by anarchist Endo Musui. What will the future of Japanese politics be? Before the establishment of the new cabinet, there is indeed a lot of excitement. (China United Press, 23rd)

(Tokyo) Due to the meeting between Prime Minister Saito and Finance Minister Takahashi, the current cabinet will indeed resign at an appropriate time, probably after the end of the Diet, the completion of the budget implementation procedures, the aftermath of the Jehol issue, and the conclusion of the withdrawal from the League of Nations. The deadline must be in July. During the meeting with the Finance Minister yesterday, the Prime Minister stated his hope that he would temporarily restrain himself before July, and the Finance Minister seemed to have understood. (Dentsu, 23rd)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saito held a meeting with Home Minister Yamamoto, the elder of the cabinet, for 20 minutes today. The Prime Minister explained the political situation and other issues, and asked the Home Minister's opinion on the issue of the cabinet's advance and retreat. The Home Minister said that the current situation is serious, so do not act rashly. The issue of advance and retreat should be taken in the same action as the other cabinet members. Prime Minister Saito plans to visit Saionji within days, convey the Home Minister's opinion, and request understanding. (Nichi-Ren, 23rd)

(Tokyo) According to observations in Japanese political circles, the elder statesmen hold a pessimistic attitude towards the future of the Saito cabinet. The reasons are roughly as follows: (1) Since Saito took office, he has indeed made considerable achievements in rescuing the emergency situation, but his facilities lack a consistent strategy. (2) The financial and economic policies do not have a long-term plan, but only make up for the current needs. The future is truly worrying. (3) Foreign Minister Uchida only stated Japan's position to European and American countries and has no constructive strategy. At a time when the situation in the Far East is becoming increasingly tense, appropriate diplomatic skills should be used to save the current isolated situation. In the future, we should actively carry out constructive diplomacy to save Japan's crisis. Based on the above reasons, the elder statesmen may not offer any consolation on the issue of Saito's resignation. However, these observations are only prevalent in the Seiyukai and the military. Other attitudes are not yet clear. (China United Press, 23rd)

Salvage experts hope the ship can be out of danger by tomorrow or Saturday. The sea is currently very calm, but there is still thick fog near the wreck site. To prevent pirate attacks, the British warship Wild Swan is still guarding the ship. (Reuters, 23rd)

Peru Takes Active Military Action

Placing Mines in Upper Amazon

Fleet Moves Directly to Colombian Coast

国民二十二日巴拉电 [巴拉 may be incorrect, unreadable here] According to a telegram from Bara on the 22nd, Peru recently had news that it would still use force to resolve the dispute over the Leticia port, disregarding the League of Nations. The ship hired a Peruvian pilot to be able to pass through the mine area. France Raises Many Objections

Progress on Four-Power Cooperation Slow

French Premier to Visit Rome

Reuters, Paris, 22nd According to Reuters in Paris on the 22nd, French Prime Minister Daladier may visit Italy within days to meet with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini to discuss the understanding of the four countries of Britain, France, Italy, and Germany. However, France has now raised many objections to this matter, which has slowed down progress. France believes that the trend of four-power understanding is sufficient to divide European countries into camps and damage the characteristics of the League of Nations. Member states of the League of Nations enjoy equal rights in the League of Nations.

Havas, Paris, 23rd According to Havas in Paris on the 23rd, when the British and French prime ministers and the diplomatic authorities of the two countries discussed the establishment of a cooperation method for the four major European powers yesterday, it was heard that French Prime Minister Daladier and French Foreign Minister Pongu had raised the following points, saying that they should be considered: (1) If the European Peace Agreement is only participated in by four strong countries, it is feared that it will divide European countries into two factions. (2) According to the League of Nations organization, all countries are equal in the meeting. If the Italian phase's new plan is followed, it is feared that the authority of the League of Nations will be harmed, as the status of the countries will be different. (3) Treaty revision is recognized by the new plan, but the possible impact of treaty revision in practice and the legal conditions for its implementation must be estimated in advance, and the countries of the Little Entente and Poland should have the right to express their opinions before the countries that advocate treaty revision. (4) If Germany is given equal treatment, what security guarantees will be given to France to reconcile? The British cabinet members all acknowledged that this plan should first be strictly studied by the French government, and the prime ministers of Britain and France plan to exchange views at length again within days.

Due to Strong Opposition from Small Countries

Military Disarmament Conference Will Not Extend

British Plan to be Proposed for Discussion Today

Reuters, Geneva, 23rd - The Geneva Military Disarmament Conference decided today not to adjourn the Military Disarmament Conference before Easter. It also voted in favor of resuming discussions on the British plan tomorrow. Today, smaller countries strongly opposed the proposal of the four major powers to adjourn the meeting, as they did not want the Rome talks to interfere with the work of the Military Disarmament Conference.

Havas, Geneva, 22nd - The declaration on the extension of the Military Disarmament Conference, jointly drafted by the Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, British Prime Minister MacDonald, and Foreign Secretary Simon, has greatly shocked people here. Some even regard this declaration as the first move by the four major European powers to interfere. Many secondary state delegations clearly stated that this matter had created a negative impression on their respective governments, and they accused the British of wanting to use the Rome and Paris talks as an excuse to extend the Disarmament Conference. It is reported that after the five major powers reached a compromise on the issue of equality of armaments last December, the General Committee did not consider it appropriate for a small number of countries to privately negotiate outside the Disarmament Conference. Yesterday's announcement by Henderson and others of the adjournment news has once again led people to suspect that the major powers will privately negotiate. Some say that Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu intends to express his views on behalf of the Little Entente countries, and Polish representative Raczkiewicz will also raise a protest again. Henderson is well aware of this sentiment, so his attitude tomorrow will be more reserved and not as straightforward as yesterday's announcement. It is likely that the adjournment will be requested by the British or Italian delegation, and Henderson will not advocate it himself. France will take a wait-and-see attitude. If the adjournment is indeed decided, the French representative will request restrictions on the length of the adjournment and that the specialized committees continue their work. Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu will soon go to Paris to state his views on behalf of the Little Entente countries.

Reuters, Athens, 22nd - The draft of the disarmament plan proposed by British Prime Minister MacDonald was approved today by a joint meeting of the Greek Prime Minister, Foreign Minister, Naval Minister, and Army Minister.

Introducing Several Japanese Naval Giants

Former Naval Minister Okada Keisuke is the leader of the Fukui Navy. On January 6th, he suddenly expressed his intention to resign, and as a result, Osumi Mineo was elected to succeed him. Osumi had previously served as a senior adjutant during Saito's tenure as Naval Minister and had also served as Vice-Minister under Okada's Naval Ministership during the Tanaka Cabinet. He was originally from the Seiyukai. If Osumi were to replace Okada in the Saito Cabinet, it would naturally be appropriate in terms of the Seiyukai.

After Okada's resignation, among the Japanese naval generals during this extraordinary period, apart from Marshal Togo of the Marshal's Office and the current Chief of Naval General Staff, Prince Fushimi Hiroyasu, Kano Kanji of the Fukui Navy is the most senior, followed by Ambo Kiyotane, Taniguchi Naomasa, Yamamoto Eisuke, and Osumi.

In Kasumigaseki (place name), the towering buildings are the gathering place of the Naval Ministry and the Naval General Staff, which control naval administration and military operations. Among them are 8,200 officers, 88,000 soldiers, more than 280 ships, and 800 aircraft. Now, let's introduce a few people.

Among the people who are considered to be naval leaders, the first thing to pay attention to is that the class of students who volunteered to enter the naval academy during the two Sino-Japanese and Russo-Japanese Wars included the largest number of naval figures in Japan.

This class of people graduated from the Naval Academy in the first term of Meiji 11, and especially focused on the 21st and 22nd terms of naval officers.

During the Donghak Party incident in Korea, Japan declared war on our country on August 1st, Meiji 27. Two months later, the current Naval Minister Osumi, of the 21st term, entered the military academy. After another two months, the 22nd term, in which Yamanashi Katsunoshin studied, was also recruited.

In Osumi's class, the most outstanding student was Tsukushi Jiro, who was promoted to Rear Admiral and then resigned. The second place was Military Councillor Yamamoto Eisuke, and the third place was Osumi. Therefore, the person who is most likely to become Naval Minister in the future should be Yamamoto. Besides Togo, Yamamoto is the leader of the Satsuma Navy, and his father is a brother of Yamamoto Gonnohyoe.

His uncle, Count Yamamoto, held the highest authority in the past Navy for a long time, and his son-in-law, Zaibe, also held the reins of the Navy for a long time. However, he was able to reach his current position entirely on his own ability and did not receive any favors from Count Yamamoto. It is rumored that the Saito Cabinet's prospects will end in May. The press has been touting Yamanashi and Kobayashi as the next Naval Minister. In today's situation, he is being promoted as a candidate for Chief of Naval General Staff. Second only to that, he should be considered the most likely to step forward.

Next, the candidate for Naval Minister is Military Councillor Yamanashi. Yamanashi was Vice-Minister of the Navy at the London Conference, opposing the activists Kato and Suetsugu of the Naval General Staff. He has considerable political skills. He was born in Sendai.

In addition to Yamamoto and Yamanashi, there is also Nomura Kichisaburo, the Commander of Yokosuka Naval District, who acts alone (i.e., the one who was injured by a Korean patriot after the Shanghai Incident), and Kobayashi Seizo, the Commander of the First Fleet. Both of these people will be promoted to Admiral this April.

Nomura and Kobayashi are different. The former has not been to the navy, but both of them are seen as naval experts in the current extraordinary era and are trusted figures of the deceased Kato Tomosaburo. Nomura served as Kato's senior adjutant and was also a member of Kato's entourage at the Washington Conference. The two were often inseparable. On the other hand, Kobayashi is Kato's nephew, so they naturally have the possibility of succeeding as ministers or chiefs. Strangely enough, the positions that these two held four or five years ago were the same, and they both maintained a mutually antagonistic position, but Nomura lost one eye, which will somewhat affect his future career. Compared to Kobayashi's career, he will inevitably be slightly inferior.

Next, we should mention Nakamura Ryuzo. Nakamura entered the military academy with the first place and graduated with the first place. He is indeed a candidate for Chief of Naval General Staff, but Suetsugu, who graduated in the same term as him, is the new leader of the entire navy and is also a candidate for Chief of Naval General Staff. This is Nakamura's formidable opponent.

Suetsugu, who suddenly became famous at the same time as the London Conference, certainly has the possibility of succeeding as the next Chief of Naval General Staff. The reason why he jumped to national fame was because he was active during the London Conference as Vice-Chief of Naval General Staff. At that time, the activities of the Naval General Staff, Chief Kato, were nothing more than decorations. In fact, it can be said that Suetsugu did everything. Perhaps Suetsugu can be promoted to Admiral at the same time as Nakamura at the end of April this year.

After Suetsugu, the leading figures are Nagano Osami of the 25th term and Sakonji Seizo, Commander of Sasebo Naval District.

Nagano was born in Tosa and has the potential to become a minister or chief. He is no less than Kobayashi, Suetsugu, and Nakamura. He served as a military attache in the United States for a long time and is an expert on the United States. Although he may become a minister, Chief of Naval General Staff is more suitable.

Sakonji's original hometown is Yonezawa, and his biological father is a lawyer living in Osaka, so he is a pure Osaka child. During his time as Commander of the Torpedo Squadron, he strongly criticized the tactics of the Naval General Staff Central, so the self-confidence of Nagano and Sakonji will soon become an important role in the Japanese Navy.

Situation at Gubeikou and Xifengkou Slightly Eases

Song Zheyuan in Ping Talks About the Combat Process

Enemies Harassing in Pingjin, Shandong, Chahar, and Suiyuan

Chiang Has Major Determination to Actively Resist the Enemy

Special Telegram from Peiping: Since the fall of Chengde, our army has fought bravely at Gubeikou and Xifengkou, leaving a page of glorious war history. At Gubeikou, the three divisions of the Northeast Army, Zhang Tingxu, He Lizhong, and Zhang Zhengfang, were originally deployed to resist the enemy, covering from Miyun and Shunyi in the south to Qingshiliang in the north, along the Great Wall. Starting on the 6th of this month, the Japanese Suzuki Brigade, in conjunction with puppet troops, launched a large-scale attack, engaging our army in fierce fighting in the Qingshiliang and Changshanyu areas. Our army fought bravely, repeatedly blunting the enemy's advance, and the enemy was unable to succeed. They then changed their strategy, sending more than 40 aircraft to Gubeikou to drop bombs, threatening our rear, while adopting flanking tactics, harassing our right flank. After several days and nights of fierce fighting, the Japanese and puppet troops suffered heavy casualties. Afterwards, the Central Army's Guan Linzheng and Huang Jie divisions went to the front line to take over the defense, and the Northeast Army gradually withdrew for rest. Unexpectedly, while our army was rotating troops, the Japanese army took the opportunity to launch a fierce attack. The Central Army came into contact with the Japanese army as soon as they arrived at the position. Since the 10th, there have been several bloody battles, with heavy casualties on both sides. Our army eventually abandoned the area outside the pass due to the sharpness of the enemy's aircraft, artillery, and tanks, and built a new position in the Nantianmen area to hold firmly to the dangerous terrain. Since the 12th, this area has entered a state of truce. At Xifengkou, the Japanese Hattori and Suzuki Brigades were severely damaged by Song Zheyuan's troops. Currently, the enemy on the Xifengkou front does not dare to face us directly. In addition to sending aircraft to our rear for reconnaissance and bombing every day, they are transferring Japanese troops and Mongolian puppet troops from Chengde and Luanping to reinforce, changing their strategy to attack Luowenyu, hoping to invade Zunhua's rear through that route. Song's troops stationed at Luowenyu also defeated the enemy, killing more than 1,000 people. On the 18th, our army circled around the enemy's rear, attacking their flanks, and the enemy was unable to support themselves, collapsing and retreating more than ten miles. Last night (19th), there was no fighting in the front. In total, at Xifengkou, from the 9th to the 19th, there were bloody battles for ten days, with more than a dozen battles of various sizes. More than 4,000 enemies were killed with broadswords, and the number killed by guns and cannons is still unknown. More than 3,000 of our soldiers also died for their country. As of today, the anti-Japanese battles at the Great Wall passes have temporarily come to a small end. Our army's defenses are also being reorganized. Two units were sent to reinforce Song's troops. At Gubeikou, troops from the He Zhuguo unit, which was responsible for the Shihu front line, were transferred to the rear, and troops from nearby were deployed to fill the gap. Commander Chiang has recently met separately with Generals Song, Han, Pang, and Wan. A new plan has been determined for the anti-Japanese military, and preparations are currently underway.

Song Zheyuan, who killed the enemy and defended against insults at Xifengkou, was summoned to Ping the night before last to meet with He Yingqin, and then went to Baoding to visit Chiang. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, he returned to Ping from Baoding. Today (20th) at 1:00 PM, he met with reporters from various newspapers at his office to report on the combat process and his meeting with Chiang. His remarks were as follows: "It is truly heartbreaking that our civilized country with 400 million people is being controlled by Japan, a small island with only tens of millions of people. This time, our country is using force against Japan because we have no other choice. Japan is determined to pursue an aggressive policy, gradually encroaching on our territory. Since the September 18th Incident, they have taken an inch and advanced a foot, their fierce flames have grown stronger, occupying the three northeastern provinces and then occupying Jinzhou and threatening Rehe. Our country can no longer tolerate it and can no longer concede, so we mobilized our troops for legitimate defense. The officers and soldiers of the various armies have all embraced the determination to resist Japan and are willing to fight the Japanese army. In peacetime, it is difficult to mobilize troops. This time, the orders arrived and they all rushed to the front line, which shows that the hearts of the people are not dead and there is something to be done to save the country. The failure of this initial Sino-Japanese war was due to the enemy's delaying tactics. After the Yuguan Incident, our army's morale should have been used in a timely manner to fight the enemy. However, because the Japanese vigorously publicized that they would not advance any further, the people were too complacent and fell into their trap. The military deployment for Rehe was delayed, which allowed the Japanese army to take advantage of the situation and enter, and Chengde was lost in less than ten days. Therefore, the failure of this Rehe war was not a defeat, but rather due to slow military deployment. On August 7th of last year, I sent a letter to Mr. Zhang Hanqing with some suggestions, asking him to prepare in time to prevent the Japanese army from invading Rehe, advocating that 50,000 people enter Rehe to garrison the Pingquan Sanjiazi area, 30,000 people guard Yuguan, and another 50,000 people serve as a reserve force in the rear. Pingquan Sanjiazi is the military center. If preparations had been made early here, even if the Japanese army came with 100,000 troops, it would probably not have been easy to cross the boundary by even a step. Even if it were not possible, it would not have been difficult to hold for a month or half a month. Unfortunately, it was not adopted at the time, and it was not until the Japanese pirates had already entered that we began to dig a well when we were already thirsty, so that the enemy's attack could not be prevented. After the Japanese army invaded Chengde, they planned to capture Xifengkou and attack Pingjin. The Japanese Hattori and Suzuki Brigades, in conjunction with Mongolian puppet troops, were ordered to occupy Xifengkou within two days. Unexpectedly, they were repelled by our army on the first day. I often say to my subordinates that we may be able to protect the country by fighting to the death. We take protecting the people as our slogan. If we cannot fight to the death and allow our compatriots to become slaves of a conquered nation, can we call it protecting the people? Some people say that those who fight on the front line are sacrifices, and those in the rear are successes. We prefer to be sacrifices and do not want to be successes. My officers and soldiers all embrace the determination to die. Although the enemy's guns and cannons are sharp, they are also useless. Since the 9th, when we came into contact with the enemy, we have repeatedly blunted the enemy's advance. The enemy could not succeed in attacking the front, so they circled around and attacked Dongjiakou on our right flank, and were severely beaten by us. Corpses were scattered all over the field. According to eyewitness accounts from the wounded soldiers, the enemy transported the corpses back in cars, with a total of 106 cars carrying six corpses each. The large number of people killed can be imagined. In the battle of Laopo Mountain, our army cut down about 600 enemy soldiers. We circled around and attacked the enemy's artillery positions, and cut down another 700 people. The enemy's infantry and cavalry units were completely wiped out. In total, after more than a dozen fierce battles of various sizes, the enemy army suffered between 3,000 and 5,000 casualties. After the fighting at Gubeikou stopped, the Japanese army concentrated its forces to attack and attack Luowenyu, intending to attack Zunhua from there and threaten the rear of Xifengkou. The enemy scouted that our troops stationed there only had one battalion, so they transferred more than 2,000 people from the 31st and 8th Regiments in Luanping, as well as more than 30 Mongolian and Korean puppet troops, and secretly attacked. Fortunately, we obtained a letter from a Japanese soldier to the captain of the 31st Regiment, peeking into their conspiracy, and quickly transferred two brigades to reinforce the defense and prepare early. Therefore, the enemy's attacks were repelled. Afterwards, the enemy again transferred reinforcements to attack, and there was hand-to-hand combat for two or three days and nights, killing many enemies. Our army also suffered considerable losses. On the night of the 18th, our army circled around and attacked the enemy's rear, and the enemy was unable to support themselves, collapsing and retreating more than ten miles. Yesterday afternoon, there was no more fighting. It is estimated that more than 1,000 people were killed and their vitality was greatly damaged. The Japanese army reported to its own country that the Japanese army's defeat in the Xifengkou area was unprecedented since the Meiji Restoration. In total, the fighting started on the 9th and lasted for ten days until yesterday (19th), and the fighting has come to a small end. The Japanese army has set up an airfield in Pingquan with about 50 to 60 aircraft to bomb our army's positions, but the effect is very small. After the war, only more than 100 of our officers and soldiers were killed or wounded by aircraft bombing. Last night at 5:00 PM, the Japanese army sent another seven aircraft to drop bombs in Zunhua City, dropping a total of more than 30 bombs, injuring only nine civilians and two soldiers. Now, our reinforcements have arrived, and with the current military strength, the enemy will definitely not be able to succeed in the Xifengkou area. However, their ambitions have not died, and they will definitely think of other ways to retaliate. Therefore, I believe that the war is still just beginning and cannot be relaxed for a day. On the bodies of Japanese artillery officers killed in action, our army found maps and plans to invade our country, not only to harass Pingjin, but also to conspire to occupy Shandong and Chahar. At this time, if we cannot use force to stop their advance and curb their ambitions, the Japanese army's ambitions will not end, and they will inevitably invade North China. The people of the country should embrace the determination to resist Japan. This time, I went to Baoding to meet with Commander Chiang to report on the situation at the front and ask for instructions. Commander Chiang has a major determination and is bound to have special plans, first to stabilize his foothold and then to advance. Citizens who die for killing the enemy, though dead, are still alive. I originally planned to return to the defense last night, but because the enemy had retreated, it was temporarily cancelled. I plan to return to the defense after discussing military matters with Minister He." (20th)

Northeast Volunteer Army Rises Up

Sitao Road is Demolished by the Volunteer Army

Volunteer Army in the Five Stations Area is Especially Active

Manchurian Defense is Empty, Japan is Unable to Manage it All

United States News Agency, Changchun, 17th - Volunteer armies in various places in Manchuria have risen up this month. Although the news is strictly censored, it is still sporadically spreading. When the Japanese troops from various places were dispatched to participate in the Battle of Rehe, the volunteer armies took the opportunity to rise up. Today (17th) at dawn, a team of volunteer army destroyed two trains on the Sitao Road, killing dozens of Japanese and Manchus, and injuring more than a hundred. The details are unknown, but according to people in the railway industry, the volunteer army demolished the railway near Ningyuan at 1:30 AM this morning. Shortly after, a train derailed at that place. Before anything could be done, the second train arrived and collided with the first train, causing numerous deaths and injuries. There are also reports of volunteer armies rising up in various places in eastern Manchuria, especially in the Five Stations area. Currently, most of the Japanese troops continue to fight in the Great Wall area, resulting in an empty defense in Manchuria. It is expected that Japan may still send troops to Manchuria. There are currently about 50,000 Japanese troops stationed in Manchuria. Many foreigners believe that Manchuria is vast, and that the Japanese will need at least 100,000 troops to maintain order there.

Fu Zuoyi's Troops

Deployed in Dolon

After Fu Consulted in Ping and Baoding, He Returned to Suiyuan and Will Take Full Responsibility for the Coming Attack and Defense

Beiping Correspondence, Fu Zuoyi, Chairman of the Suiyuan Provincial Government, recently went to Baoding to meet with Commander Chiang to ask for instructions, and after returning to Ping, he has been in consultations with He Yingqin for several days. Now that everything is done, today (20th), he is taking a car back to Zhangjiakou with Secretary-General Zeng Chunfu and more than a dozen attendants. Before leaving, Fu made the following remarks to reporters at the station: "I had to make a small stay in Beiping and Baoding because I had to ask Commander Chiang for important national defense matters. Because defense is important, I must return to the defense immediately. It is the duty of a soldier to defend against insults and defend the land, so I must work hard and take full responsibility. The open army is currently in Dolon, and the defense is extremely solid. The area is commonly known as Lama Temple, located in the upper reaches of the Wan River, where the four reaches of Inner and Outer Mongolia meet, and it was opened as a commercial port in the third year of the Republic of China. The prosperity of the business is comparable to that of Zhangjiakou, and it is a large metropolis in southern Mongolia," and so on. (20th)

He Chengjun Stationed in Ping

Assisting in the Anti-Japanese Military Effort

The Xi'an Executive Office Temporarily Abolished

To Immediately Transfer to Hankou to Suppress Bandits in Jiangxi

Hankou Correspondence: He Chengjun, the Pacification Director stationed in Hubei, who was recently stationed in Xi'an to oversee the suppression of the bandit Xu, once expressed his intention to shift his troops to resist foreign aggression after the remaining bandits were eliminated. Recently, Bazhong and Nanjiang were successively recovered by Tian Songyao's forces, and the remaining bandits are expected to be eradicated. He was summoned by telegram by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to consult on all matters. Consequently, on the 16th, he departed from Xi'an for Tongguan, passed through Zhengzhou on the 17th, and arrived in Baoding on the 18th to meet with Chiang. He learned that Chiang had specially ordered He to be stationed in Peiping to assist in the major plan of resisting Japan. The Xi'an Executive Office was temporarily abolished. After receiving the order, He took a train to Peiping from Baoding on the 21st. He dispatched Senior Staff Officer Xu Chengxi to inspect the Xifengkou area, and telegraphed Chief of Staff Zhu Chuanjing to lead the personnel of the Xi'an Executive Office back to Hankou. All bandit suppression military affairs were handed over to Yang Hucheng, the Pacification Director stationed in Shaanxi, and Tian Songyao, the Bandit Suppression Supervisor of the Sichuan-Shaanxi Border Region, for their responsibility. As the national crisis is severe, the generals under He's leadership stationed in Hubei, such as Xu Yuanquan, Wei Lihuang, Qian Dajun, Xiao Zhichu, and Zhang Zhenhan, are all vying to request Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for permission to fight the enemy. It is reported that a certain division has been ordered to depart, and a military station has been established to facilitate transportation. [Unintelligible] is appointed as the general supervisor, and [Unintelligible] is appointed as the deputy supervisor. [Unintelligible] are respectively appointed as the heads of the accounting and logistics departments. A total of fifteen vehicles have been allocated along the Xianghua, Hankou, and Yichang roads, awaiting requisition. Although Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is in the north, presiding over the anti-Japanese military affairs, he is also extremely concerned about the bandit suppression in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces, and has entrusted the authority of the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the three provinces to Liu Zhi, the Pacification Director stationed in Henan, to act as his agent. It is reported that Liu will arrive in Hankou within days, but as the focus of bandit suppression is in Jiangxi, he may not stay in Hankou and will proceed directly to Nanchang to supervise the bandit suppression. (March 22nd)

Han Fuqu

Returning to Jinan After Meeting Chiang in Baoding

Seeking Instructions on Strategies from Chiang

No Political Matters Were Discussed

Jinan Correspondence: Han Fuqu left Jinan yesterday, passing through Tianjin and Peiping, and arrived in Baoding on the 20th to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. He consulted on many matters regarding the overall situation. That evening, he returned to Peiping and transferred to Tianjin. Today (the 21st) at 9:00 AM, Han, along with Ge Guangting and others, took a special train from Tianjin southward. At 3:00 PM, the train arrived at Sangyuan. He immediately used the telephone to notify the magistrate of Dezhou County and Qiao Lizhi, the commander of the 74th Division, to order military and government personnel and gather the people at the station to await his speech upon arrival in Dezhou. At 4:00 PM, the train arrived in Dezhou. Qiao Lizhi led the division's Chief of Staff Yin Zuxiong, Brigade Commander Ma Guanyi, County Magistrate Li Shude, along with dozens of government officials and officers, and a squad of soldiers, to welcome him at the station. After alighting from the train, Han first reviewed the troops welcoming him at the station, and then summoned Qiao Lizhi and Ma Guanyi onto the train to give instructions. At the same time, he ordered all troops, personnel from various agencies, and civilians stationed in Dezhou to gather at the large parade ground next to the station to listen to his speech. The general idea of his speech was to encourage the military and civilians to act in unison and move towards the path of patriotism. After the speech, the special train continued southward. After passing Yucheng, Jinan had already received a telephone report. Personnel from various Party, government, and military agencies all arrived at the station to welcome him. At 8:55 PM, he arrived in Jinan. Han, along with Ge Guangting, Zhang Liancheng, Yao Yijie, and Zhang Shouqian, all disembarked from the train. Liu Xizhong remained in Peiping. Han then spoke to reporters, briefly saying, "My impression of this trip to Peiping and Baoding is very good. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is determined to strive to resist to the end. In military terms, everything at the front is now arranged by Minister He, which is very tight, with deep trenches and high walls waiting for the enemy. The fighting at Xifengkou was very good, and there was not much fighting at Gubeikou. Although there have been small clashes recently, there have been no major battles. I met with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, reported on the military and political situation in this province, and sought instructions on strategies. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek ordered me to hurry back, prepare everything in order, and maintain the public order of this province. Political matters were not discussed. I met with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek once at 8:15 AM yesterday morning, and again after 12:00 PM. After lunch, I left Baoding at 3:00 PM and went to Peiping, to Minister He's place, and had dinner at Chairman Wan's (Fulin) place. After passing through Tianjin, I met with Chairman Yu (Xuezhong). I took a train back from Tianjin again this morning. As for other matters that cannot be disclosed, please forgive me." (March 21st)

Cai Tingkai

Preparing for the Anti-Japanese Military Effort

Red Bandits in Tai'ning Retreat Backwards

Overseas Chinese Donate Four Aircraft to Fujian

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Red bandits on the border between northern Fujian and eastern Jiangxi have been repeatedly attacked by large Fujian and Jiangxi armies. The total number of remaining bandits is only over 30,000, and they have been divided into two groups: one gathered between Zixi, Lichuan, Guangze, and Tai'ning; and the other gathered between Shicheng, Ruijin, Ninghua, and Changting, constructing defensive works in an attempt to resist stubbornly for a long time. Recently, taking advantage of the concentration of Fujian troops [Unintelligible] preparing to attack [Unintelligible], they transferred troops from the Zixi and Lichuan areas and invaded Guangze and Tai'ning. Therefore, starting on March 15th, fierce battles began with the Jiang Yan Brigade of the Liu Division stationed in Tai'ning and the Zhou Zhiqian Division stationed in Guangze. By the 17th, the bandit forces on the Tai'ning front were unable to withstand the pressure and retreated along the original route to Lichuan. On the Guangze front, the bandit forces were larger, and they held out for many days. On the 19th, troops stationed in Shaowu rushed to their rescue, and the bandits collapsed and retreated. Cai Tingkai, the commander-in-chief of the 19th Route Army, went to Zhangzhou in early this month to command the bandit suppression military affairs in western Fujian. On the 19th, he returned to the province by plane from Zhangzhou with Deng Shizeng, the chief of staff of the Pacification Headquarters. It is reported that they are preparing for the anti-Japanese military effort. The staff office of the Pacification Headquarters summoned reporters from various newspapers in the city for a conversation, generally stating that in this tense situation, the deployment and actions of the troops going north to resist Japan should be reported with caution to avoid leaking secrets. In addition, the training regiment of the 61st Division of the 19th Army stationed in the province and the students of the defense corps cadre training school have been conducting camping and field exercises on the hills outside the northwest gates for days. The security police team of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau and the police trainees of the police training school are also conducting street fighting and night combat exercises in the streets and alleys of the northwest districts of the city at night, which is extremely busy. As for the aircraft donated to the 19th Route Army by overseas Chinese in the Philippines, four have been transported. On the 18th, they flew from Xiamen to the provincial capital and were placed at the Wangzhuang airfield. Yesterday and today, they were piloted by members of the aviation team of the Pacification Headquarters, soaring in the sky for test flights. (March 20th)

Tan Yingzhu, a Prominent Communist Leader, Returns to Hunan to Surrender

Claims to Have Participated in Bandit Suppression Work in Southern Fujian Long Ago

Currently Under Custody of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters Awaiting Disposition

Changsha Correspondence: Before the May 21st Incident, the figures who caused great terror throughout Hunan were the Communist leaders Guo Liang, Xia Xi, Tan Yingzhu, and Yi Lirong. Guo Liang was arrested in Yueyang in 1928, escorted to the provincial capital, and executed. The whereabouts of the others have been unknown for the past five or six years. Among them, Tan Yingzhu, a native of Liuyang, served as the chairman of the General Labor Union before the May 21st Incident, commanding the peasant and worker self-defense army. Xu Kexiang launched the Communist purge in Changsha on May 21st, which was to eliminate the power of Tan and others in Hunan. Due to their defeat, Tan and others fled the province. Cheng Qian, Lu Diping, and He Jian successively presided over the administration of Hunan, all offering a reward of three thousand yuan and issuing public arrest warrants, but they were never apprehended. Last winter, Tan's wife, Huang Yonglan, returned to the province from Shanghai to celebrate her mother's birthday. She was suddenly arrested by the Changsha County Government and presented to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters. She was repeatedly interrogated and ordered to hand over her husband, Tan Yingzhu, but she firmly refused to reveal his whereabouts. The case has been suspended for several months without a resolution. Unexpectedly, at 10:00 AM on the 17th of this month, Tan suddenly went to the Hunan Bandit Suppression Headquarters in person, requested to see He Jian, the concurrent commander, and requested to surrender. At that time, He was not at the headquarters, so Executive Director Li Qiongyan entered and interviewed him. After everything, he was handed over to the special service team for custody, awaiting He Jian's disposition. When all circles heard of this, they were all surprised. According to Tan's confession to Li Qiong, he left the Communist Party in 1927 after escaping from Changsha in May 1927, and did a lot of bandit suppression work in Zhang Zhen's office in Fujian. This time, he came to the province this morning after passing through Shanghai and Hankou from Fujian, and came to the headquarters to surrender, etc. It is still unknown how He will dispose of him. The text of Tan's surrender submission is recorded as follows: "A submission regarding returning to Hunan to surrender and requesting permission to surrender according to law. I, originally named Tan Yingzhu, after the Changsha May 21st Incident occurred and the Kuomintang and Communists split, left the Communist Party, changed my name to Li Jian, registered at the Longxi County Branch of the Chinese Kuomintang in Fujian, and submitted it to the Central Executive Committee, which issued Party Certificate No. Min Zi 02790. I have participated in bandit suppression work in the southern Fujian area. However, at that time, military affairs were rushed, and southern Fujian was located in a remote area. There were no clear regulations on the legal procedures for public surrender, and I had been away from Hunan for a long time, so I was even more estranged from the situation in Hunan. For many years in office, I only knew to be loyal to the Three Principles of the People and to work hard in bandit suppression, and I thought that since I belonged to the Kuomintang, there would be no other problems. In addition, military affairs bound me, and I could not return to Hunan. Unfortunately, after my wife, Huang Yonglan, arrived in Hunan last winter, I was arrested and imprisoned by the Changsha County Government because I had participated in the Communist Party before. When the incident occurred, my wife, Huang Yonglan, was far away thousands of miles away, and it was difficult to arrive in the morning and arrive in the evening. Also, she did not know whether I could collect all the documents of participating in bandit suppression in Fujian over the years, and it was inconvenient to confess the truth due to the circumstances at the time. I have learned of this so far, so I especially ask Zhang Zhen, the commander of the 49th Division of the Army, to prepare a document detailing my years of bandit suppression work in Fujian and send it to your department for verification. I have brought it here after arriving in the province today. I respectfully submit it to your department, and I respectfully request permission to surrender according to law. I respectfully request instructions on how to handle the surrender procedures, so that there will be a follow-up, which will be very helpful. Respectfully submitted to He, Commander of the Hunan Bandit Suppression Headquarters." Attached is the approval order No. Can Zi 12 from the Headquarters of the 49th Division of the Army, a letter No. Can Zi 13, a certificate No. Dang Zi 114 from the Teachers Examination Committee of the Longxi County Party Branch, an instruction No. Can Zi 402 from the Fujian Bandit Suppression Headquarters, an instruction No. Mi Zi 204, an instruction No. Can Zi 336, an official letter from the Temporary First Division of the Army Special Party Office entrusting the Acting Organization Department Director, and an appointment letter from the 49th Division of the Army appointing the leader of the Bandit Suppression Propaganda Brigade. (March 18th)

Songjiang

Preparing to Dredge the City River

The city's river channels were dredged ten years ago, resulting in a gradual silting up over the years. Every time the tide recedes, the riverbed is fully exposed, and shallow boats run aground and cannot pass. This greatly affects the transportation of the city's commerce and industry. Residents also rely entirely on river water for their drinking water. During repeated fires, the dry river and shallow water have led to sighs of helplessness. The citizens' hope for dredging is like expecting clouds during a great drought. The county government previously received an order from the province to organize a committee for dredging the river by conscription. The First District Office had previously resolved to prepare for dredging the city river at the district affairs meeting. However, in the past, dredging the river involved levying a storefront donation and hiring laborers to pay according to the amount of earthwork. There were still concerns that it would not be enough. The result of the last dredging was that the government had to subsidize a considerable amount and borrow money from the financial sector to cope, which has not yet been repaid. If the provincial method of conscripting labor is followed, although a substitute fee can be collected, it is feared that the amount collected will be less than half of the storefront donation, making it even more difficult to start. The authorities still need to convene local people to discuss in detail what method to take for dredging the river. The district office has scheduled a meeting, hoping to start construction soon to satisfy the people's expectations.

Wuxi

Township Head Kidnapped in the Third District

Han Wentai, the head of Xu Xie Township in the northern part of Zhouxin Town, Third District of the county, whose family residence is at Lucun Bridge, has some property. At about 3:00 AM the day before yesterday, more than a dozen bandits suddenly came, carrying quick-firing guns and flashlights, climbed over the high walls and entered the house, searching and looting everywhere. Before leaving, they kidnapped the victim, Han Wentai. Afterwards, the victim's Tongtu chief reported to the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau and the Zhouxin Town Security Corps. Police officers were immediately dispatched to pursue the bandits, but they had already fled far away and could not be captured.

Military Police Corps Captures Lake Bandits

The monitoring director of the Fifth Military Police Corps stationed in Wuxi recently received a secret report that a Taihu bandit leader, due to the Jiangzhe water police's intense encirclement and suppression, was hiding in the mountains along the lake. He immediately ordered a special service team to go to the destination with informants to conduct a search. Two bandit leaders were captured on the spot and sent to the corps headquarters. They confessed that there were many followers and that they had committed many crimes. The remaining accomplices are currently being searched for in order to eradicate the roots.

Private Possession of Military Weapons Detained for Investigation

The military police stationed in Wuxi arrested Yang Genxiang, Liu Xikang, Zhang Asan, and others at the Fuxing Leather Suitcase Shop in Shuyuan Lane in the city the night before last, and seized a pistol and a package of bullets. According to Liu Xikang's confession, the pistol was borrowed from Zhu Peiyu, who currently lives in the Suyemi Rice Shop outside the West Gate. Zhu Peiyu was also arrested that night and sent to the corps headquarters. After interrogation, it was learned that Zhu had previously served as a drill instructor in the merchant corps. The gun was picked up in Huishan during the Jiazi Year Qilu War and had not been registered. He confirmed that he had lent it to Liu and others for use. Corps Commander Lan ordered Liu and others to be detained for private possession of military weapons and to await investigation.

Changzhou

Director of the Department of Education Visits Changzhou

Zhou Fohai, the director of the Department of Education of Jiangsu Province, recently went to Danyang to inspect education. At about 7:00 PM on the 22nd, he arrived in Changzhou by special express train from Danyang. County Magistrate Zhang Pengzhu and Director of the Bureau of Education Yang Haoming, upon hearing the news, went to the station to greet him in advance. After getting off the train, he went to the Provincial Changzhong for dinner and inspected the students' self-study class. Those who came with him this time included Chen Zhidong, the head of the Second Section, Xiang Jutan, the head of the Third Section, and Yi Junzuo, the director of compilation and review. They all stayed at the Dacheng Hotel. On the 23rd, he inspected various educational institutions. It was scheduled to convene teachers and staff of various schools at the Provincial Changzhong on the 24th for instructions. He is expected to go to Wuxi for inspection around the 25th.

Zhenjiang

Canal Works Bureau Issues Mortgage Bonds

The Jiangbei Canal Works Bureau, due to the need for a large amount of funds for the crushed stone project on the western embankment of the canal, submitted a request to the Finance and Construction Departments to issue Jiangbei Canal Works mortgage bonds to provide urgent relief. The provincial departments have approved the request and allocated it to various counties along the canal. It is reported that half of the amount will be deducted from the provincial and county road construction mu tax.

Eight County Farms Under the Jurisdiction of the Department of Education

The agricultural promotion centers in Danyang, Yixing, Baoshan, Qidong, Funing, Lianshui, Suqian, and Ganxian have been designated by the provincial government to be under the jurisdiction of the Department of Education in order to seek practical experience in livelihood education. Yesterday, a special order was issued to the governments of the respective counties to separately register the farms, economics, farmland, equipment, documents, and industrial funds, both received and unreceived, and hand them over to the Bureau of Education for acceptance, so that the bureau can plan and manage them as soon as possible. In counties where the Bureau of Education has been abolished, the county government is responsible for planning and implementing the project.

Jiangsu Province Will Establish Administrative Supervision

The call for Jiangsu Province to establish a chief county magistrate was very loud last autumn. However, due to the Japanese invasion of Shanghai, it was temporarily shelved and not implemented. It is now learned that the provincial government has re-proposed it and plans to change the name to Administrative Supervision Office, based on the methods of Hubei and Henan provinces. Fifteen supervisors will be appointed throughout the province. Seven supervisors will be appointed first soon. The county magistrate where the office is located will be concurrently served by the supervisor. Some say that the supervisor will not concurrently serve as the county magistrate. The system is like the former Daoyin, but the jurisdiction is smaller and the number of supervisors is larger. As for the candidates for supervisors, it is said that most of them will be borrowed from members of the Control Yuan or current, more capable county magistrates. The date of implementation will not be later than mid-April.

Qingpu

Aviation Patriotic Movement Assembly

At 9:00 AM on the 19th of this month, the county party headquarters convened various agencies, organizations, schools, local officials, and people from all walks of life in the city to hold an aviation patriotic and thrift movement propaganda meeting. On that day, about 1,000 people attended. Chairman Guo and County Magistrate Yu delivered speeches at the meeting. Their words were inspiring and moving to the listeners. Special publications and picture newspapers were distributed on the spot to broaden the propaganda. The meeting did not disperse until 11:00 AM.

Yangzhou

Fire at Lampshade Factory, Four People Burned to Death

Yesterday (the 21st) morning at 5:00 AM, at the Meiji Xinghua Lampshade Factory in Henan outside the Customs Office, the gas cylinder suddenly exploded, and the fire spread in all directions, immediately piercing the roof. All three tile houses and half of the thatched houses were reduced to ashes. When the fire started, most of the workers in the factory were still asleep. Four child laborers, Xuan Xiao, Chen Xiaoyang, Wang Xiaoheshang, and Wang Changlin, were unable to escape and were buried in the fire. Six workers, Xiao Gu, Xiao Ma, Bai Yuanyuan, Long Sifu, Chen Bikuo, and Xiao Caizi, were burned. The factory is now trying to deal with the aftermath and has requested the procuratorate to send personnel to investigate.

Nantong

Thorough Investigation of the Soil Dredging Theft Case

A large package of opium was found in the Jiangmian River of Liuhai Sand Thirteen Weigang in Nantong. It was salvaged by Huang Dazhang and others. During the transfer of the 16 opium cakes by the Public Security Bureau, they suddenly became mud cakes. The provincial government has ordered the county government to thoroughly investigate the situation based on the report filed by the original informant. The prosecutor's office of the county court summoned Du Yutian, the director of the Public Security Bureau of the district, for questioning twice, and handed Du over to the county bureau for custody. It also filed a public prosecution with the criminal court.

Lin Biao Will Visit Northern Jiangsu to Inspect

Lin Biao, the president of the Jiangsu Higher Court, will come to the counties of Tongruhai in northern Jiangsu within days to inspect the judiciary and give instructions on the expansion of the Fourth Prison.

Gaoyou

Corps Commander Arrested for Being a Bandit

Gao Tianjue, the Corps Commander of the Yanxing Security Corps of Lu Wangzhuang, Ninth District of the county, led more than a dozen bandits armed with sharp weapons to Yang Zheng's house, a wealthy household in Cunxia, the day before yesterday afternoon, and kidnapped his eldest son, who was in his twenties. Yang immediately went forward to snatch him back, but was chopped off his wrist by Gao Tuanzong with a sharp weapon. Yang then reported to the first squadron of the 25th team of the Provincial Public Security Corps stationed at Nangantuo. Squadron Leader Li Baichuan immediately led his team to the scene. The hostage was gone. Gao Tianjue and his son were taken into custody. Squadron Leader Li plans to send the suspect to the brigade headquarters for interrogation.

Huzhou

Night Shift Between Huzhou and Hangzhou Robbed by Bandits

The night shift boat between Huzhou and Hangzhou of the Ning Shao Lun Bureau left Hangzhou for Huzhou at about 4:00 PM on the 20th. When passing through the Anqing Bridge area of Deqing, Huzhou, a bandit boat suddenly came. More than a dozen bandits each held pistols and fired several shots at the boat, shouting for it to stop. They swarmed onto the boat and looted it. All forty-plus passengers on the boat and tugboat were searched one by one, without exception. The total loss was more than a thousand yuan.
