The Story of the Theft of Guo Chengen's Family's Valuable Silver Pagoda

Stolen in the Dark of Night by Former Servants

Sold at a Good Price, with the Large Sum Remitted to Tianjin

Although the Pagoda Was Dismantled, It Fortunately Returned to Its Original Owner

Both Brothers Each Sentenced to Three Years of Imprisonment

Guo Chengen, director of the Central Mint, formerly served as director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration. Upon his departure, colleagues from the two railway administrations presented him with a seven-foot silver pagoda as a memento. This pagoda was not only exceptionally tall but also exquisitely carved. It was said to be worth 2,000 gold pieces. Guo cherished it greatly and placed it in the hall of his residence at 775 Changping Road in western Shanghai, protected by glass windows, making it visible but inaccessible. Unexpectedly, before dawn on the third day of this week, this treasured memento suddenly disappeared. After the family members noticed it in the morning, they immediately reported it to Mr. Guo, who sent a messenger to report to the Gordon Road Police Station and request an investigation. The detective chief dispatched Chinese and foreign detectives, including Cai Liu, and officer No. 324 to investigate the Guo residence first, and then launched a four-way investigation. Within a few hours, they recovered both the people and the stolen goods, and the pagoda was returned to its original owner. The thieves, named Xing Yangxu and Xing Keming, were brothers from Tianjin, currently residing at 9, Lane 603, Kang Nao Tu Road. Yangxu was originally a former servant of Guo's residence, but was dismissed by the owner for some reason a few months ago and has been unemployed ever since. Recently, Yangxu returned to Guo's residence, expressing his willingness to serve and begging to be rehired, but Mr. Guo ultimately refused. Disappointed, he conceived the idea of stealing the pagoda. On the morning of the 22nd of this month at around 2:00 AM, he and his brother Keming sneaked into Guo's residence at night. The house was surrounded by bamboo fences. The Xing brothers climbed over the fence and suddenly saw three dogs guarding the house squatting in the open space outside the door, barking wildly at the shadows. Fearing being bitten by the dogs, the Xing brothers retreated and purchased three pieces of cake from a nearby food store, bringing them back and feeding them to the dogs. The three dogs then fell silent. Xing realized that the dogs had been tamed and went into the house to take out burglary tools, prying open the glass window protecting the pagoda. However, because the pagoda was very tall, they could not carry it. They dismantled the pagoda and took out the sections one by one, making several trips before they had stolen everything. In addition to the pagoda, they also stole three coats and tablecloths. At 8:00 AM in the morning, the two thieves took the stolen goods to Room 29 of the Huadong Apartment at 54 Jinyi Lane, Malong Road, in the French Concession to rest. Coincidentally, Mr. A, an assistant to Detective Jin Jiuling of the Lujiawan Police Station, also lived in the apartment. He caught a glimpse of the pagoda and found it suspicious, so he paid attention to it. Not long after the two thieves rested, they took the pagoda out again. Mr. A followed them directly to the Wupin Pawnshop at 462 Gongguan Road and saw the two thieves entering to sell the pagoda. Mr. A immediately reported to Detective Jin and went to investigate and arrest them. By this time, the Xing brothers had already sold the pagoda to the pawnshop for a total price of 311 yuan. They pawned the coats at three pawnshops on Malong Road, Shunxing, Wangzhi Road, Xiexing, and Sapesai Road, Hexing, for a price of 16 yuan. They returned to the apartment and were arrested. The original stolen goods were recovered from each pawnshop. The Gordon Road Police Station was notified, and the Xing brothers were taken back to the police station along with the stolen goods. This morning, witnesses were gathered, and the two were sent to the First Special District District Court. Judge Qian Wenji conducted the preliminary hearing. After the police lawyer Wang Yaotang explained the circumstances of the case, he stated that the stolen money obtained by the defendants, according to their confession, had been given to the Baxian Branch of Chongdetang for remittance to Tianjin in the amount of 280 yuan. The police immediately sent detectives to the branch to investigate and learned that it had already been remitted by the head office. They then visited the postmaster, who agreed to immediately send a telegram to detain the funds for return. A letter should be prepared and given to the detectives to go to the post office to retrieve the funds and hand them over to the owner. When questioned, the defendant Xing Yangxu admitted to the theft but stated that his brother did not go with him during the theft, but they went together during the sale of the stolen goods. Xing Keming's confession was roughly the same. After the trial, Judge Qian sentenced both defendants to three years of imprisonment, and the stolen goods were ordered to be returned to the original owner.

Assassination Case on Malong Road This Morning

The Deceased Was Originally a Fudan University Student from Nanxi

Currently Serving as an Adjutant in the Eastern Sichuan Border Defense Headquarters

Came to Shanghai to Marry a Female Classmate and Suddenly Suffered a Tragedy

At around 9:00 AM this morning, a young man in a suit was suddenly assassinated in front of No. 54 Puqing Lane, Malong Road, in the French Concession. The details are as follows:

Young Man Shot Dead

At around 9:00 AM this morning, a gunshot suddenly rang out at the entrance of Puqing Lane, Malong Road, Bailaini Meng, French Concession. Residents in the lane did not pay attention at first, but then a young man in a suit was found lying in a pool of blood in front of No. 54. The young man had been shot in the back of the head behind his left ear, the bullet had not pierced through. The entire lane was immediately in an uproar. The lane manager immediately reported it to the police station.

Fudan University Student

The police chief immediately ordered detectives to rush to the scene for investigation. However, the young man had been dead for a long time. The body was then taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall morgue for an autopsy. A letter from Fudan University was found in the deceased's pocket. The detectives then went to Fudan University to investigate. It was confirmed that the deceased was indeed a student of the school. The deceased's fellow student and friend, Zhang Rong, personally went to the morgue to identify the body.

Currently Serving as an Adjutant

According to Zhang Rong, the deceased's name was Du Nanxi, 26 years old, from Shizhu County, Sichuan Province. His original surname was Chen, and the deceased was the third son. He was adopted by his maternal grandfather's family, the Du family, at a young age. His eldest brother, Chen Lanting, is currently the commander and division commander of the Eastern Sichuan Border Defense. His second brother, Guangting, previously served as a regimental commander under his brother and died of illness in 1931. At that time, the deceased was studying at Fudan University. Upon hearing the news of his brother's death, he returned to Sichuan in October of that year and served as an adjutant in the Eastern Sichuan Border Defense Headquarters.

Met a Female Classmate

The deceased initially graduated from Jiangbei Zhiping Middle School in Chongqing. In the spring of 1928, he came to Shanghai and studied on his own for half a year. After the summer vacation of that year, he went to Nanjing and audited courses at Central University for a year. In the autumn of 1929, he entered Fudan University, majoring in municipal administration. At that time, a female classmate named Ding Yandao, from Jinshan Zhujing, developed a close relationship with the deceased and became engaged.

Came to Shanghai to Get Married

After the deceased returned to Sichuan, he served as an adjutant in the Eastern Sichuan Border Defense Headquarters until the 21st of this month, when he took a plane from Hankou to Shanghai. It is reported that this trip to Shanghai was specifically to marry Ding Yandao. At 8:00 AM this morning, he left the school to visit friends and said that he would return to school before lunch. Unexpectedly, he was assassinated and would never return. The deceased's old mother is still alive, and her grief upon hearing this tragic news can be imagined.

Opportunity for People to Do Good Things Ji

In today's world of rampant and tyrannical actions and the destruction of justice, if a nation encounters foreign aggression and does not have the determination to make the greatest sacrifices and engage in great and heroic struggles to cross the vast sea of ​​suffering and desperately seize justice from the clutches of tyranny, then undoubtedly the nation's life and soul will be lost and disappear along with the iron hooves of the oppressor. Moreover, in the struggle for survival of the fittest, if a nation's life force is already in the hands of the oppressor, and it still fantasizes about "turning over," there is certainly hope, unless it waits for the outbreak of a world revolution. However, a world revolution also requires one to have a greater and more intense determination to sacrifice, so that one can seize the "good opportunity" and not let it pass by.

As soon as the clutches of the violent Japanese army extended to the border of Rehe, the troops like the extremely shameless Tang department were frightened out of their wits and retreated repeatedly, finally abandoning Chengde without hearing the sound of gunfire. The remaining power of the violent Japanese army has not yet dissipated, and the overall situation seems to be hopeless. Unexpectedly, when the good news arrived, Sun Dianying's troops dared to fight a desperate battle as an isolated army beyond the Great Wall without being ordered by the headquarters, in order to blunt the enemy's sharp edge and stabilize our front. Subsequently, Song Zheyuan's troops, with "three divisions united like family," dared to take the offensive and won many victories. Recently, newspapers also reported that "Sun Dianying's troops will request an order for a full-scale counterattack, and their troops are willing to be the pioneers to recapture Chengde. What a piece of good news!" Strange! Why did Sun Dianying's troops, which are not usually noticed, suddenly have such a heroic spirit to swallow the Milky Way? When asked strangely, they said: "Today is a good opportunity for us to do good things" (see the reports of the 20th). After listening happily, we can easily imagine that they not only have the determination to make the greatest sacrifices and the spirit of fighting, but also have a unique vision to see through the cycle of tooth for tooth and eye for eye in the internal strife of the past 21 years, with each fratricidal war costing countless lives. And those who are inhumane butchers, under the command of the slaughterhouse bosses, have experienced this inhuman slaughterhouse, which is naturally not "a good opportunity for people to do good things," that is, not even the basic "way of being human," which is very clear. Now that we hear Mr. Sun's bells and drums, can we not feel guilty before the gods, suddenly awaken, quickly point our guns at the violent army to build a miracle and redeem our past sins?

Without experiencing wind and frost, one does not know the strength of pine and cypress. Mr. Sun can recognize that fighting against the violent Japanese army and counterattacking Rehe is "a good opportunity for people to do good things," which clearly means standing on the position of the entire nation's interests and not hesitating to sacrifice oneself to fight against imperialism. Once this message is broadcast, if it can inspire the troops of the whole country to rise up in response, then the triumphal song of final victory will surely spread frequently from beyond the Great Wall!

Using the Dead? Xingzhu

丨Countless Filial Sons and Virtuous Grandchildren丨

"A dead girl is a good girl." This is a popular saying in our hometown. So in this era, it is easier to be praised or supported after death. Otherwise, before one's natural death, one is often attacked and even hoped to die sooner rather than later.

We only need to look at the wealthy and famous people. Once their parents die, they will expand their publicity to express their condolences. First, they send out obituaries, using all their life's efforts to describe how good the living children and grandchildren are, what rank they hold, where their names are known, and what important positions they have held... It's as if each family member's resume is, in the final analysis, all thanks to the parents' education. It's truly a family blessed with intelligence and beauty. Therefore, the children's grief over their parents' passing is a small matter. Taking this opportunity to publicize their own achievements, qualifications, and knowledge to the public is a work that cannot be ignored. Also, the parents' bodies, placed in coffins, should be buried, but because they want to show off, they specially hire many people to carry the coffin and parade it through the streets, walking through the bustling streets, displaying many ornaments, and wishing they could take out all the banknotes in the bank and stick them on their mourning clothes. Moreover, deeply afraid that others will misunderstand that they are not filial sons and virtuous grandchildren, they pay special attention to wailing, being supported by their families and walking slowly step by step to show that such descendants are not only wealthy but also filial, and can even enter the Confucian Temple and have a filial piety arch erected.

In fact, when the parents were alive, they may have been scolded for being stubborn for arranging marriages or were considered misers for not giving enough money for the children and grandchildren to spend, and scolded for being old and not dying... However, once they die, the parents become wise parents, and the descendants also become filial descendants. The dead are gone, and they may not care much. The living, however, use the dead to show off themselves, which seems to be a right that the descendants should enjoy. Ah! Ah! So don't blame the fact that since ancient times, many idols have been made using the dead.

However, there are also exceptions. Those who are executed by the government because they have been shot or beheaded have committed unspeakable crimes. Although they are dead, no one praises them as good people. Does this prove that the executions were correct?

Various Government Organizations

Not Allowed to Travel by Train on Credit

Order from the National Government to All Agencies

(Nanjing) Railway Minister Gu Mengyu presented to the Executive Yuan, which forwarded it to the National Government, stating that various government organizations are directly requesting the Railway Bureau to allow them to travel or transport public goods on credit. As a result, the Railway Bureau is directly sending letters to various organizations requesting appropriations, which violates the administrative system and the Railway Department's efforts to regulate the procedures for government personnel traveling on credit. It should be requested that the National Government and the Executive Yuan issue a general order to all subordinate organizations, instructing them not to directly request the Railway Bureau to allow them to travel or transport public goods on credit in the future, in order to maintain railway administration. According to the report, the National Government issued an order to all government organizations on the 23rd. (Central News Agency dispatch on the morning of the 24th)

Rong Zhen Summoned to Baoding

(Beiping) Rong Zhen, summoned by Chiang Kai-shek, is scheduled to go to Baoding this morning to meet with him. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

German Chancellor Hitler

Announces Diplomatic Policy

Strongly Denies Responsibility for the European War

Equality and Freedom as the Only Requirements

Enthusiastic Support for the Italian Plan

Maintains Friendly Relations with Russia

Parliament Passes a Bill Authorizing the Government to Have Dictatorial Powers

Reuter's, Berlin, 23rd - Today, Chancellor Hitler announced the policy of the National Socialist government in a speech to Parliament. He strongly denied Germany's responsibility for the European War and stated that the arsonist of the Reichstag and his accomplices would be publicly executed in the shortest possible time. Supporters of the government cheered loudly upon hearing this. After the cheering subsided, Hitler added that the current government is determined to eradicate the power of the German Communist Party in Germany and will not allow outside interference. As for the restoration of the empire, it will be considered in the future, and there is currently no need for it. If the states solve this problem on their own, such actions will be regarded as acts of undermining German unity. Germany will treat all religions fairly, but acts of treason will be dealt with by "savage and cruel" means. Germany has fully fulfilled its obligations under the Treaty of Versailles. The reconstruction of German warships is only taking place on a small scale. Military equipment is inadequate, and the army organization is incomplete. If other countries actively fulfill their obligations for disarmament, the German government will not increase its troops. Germany's only demands are equality and freedom. Germany is willing to share the blessings of peace with the world and therefore strongly prevents the countries of the world from being divided into several categories. Any country that is willing to abandon old evils and start a new life, Germany is willing to join hands with it. Hitler also said that common sense should be applied to the organization of commerce and the cancellation of reparations and war debts. Regarding Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's plan to establish an understanding among Germany, France, Britain, and Italy, Hitler said that if the governments of Germany and France can completely resolve the various problems between the two countries, then a kind of understanding can be established between Germany and France. Hitler also said that Mussolini's policy for ensuring European peace and development is very far-sighted, and we attach great importance to this plan and are prepared to cooperate with it in order to promote peaceful cooperation among Germany, France, Italy, and Britain. Germany should do its best for this, because this matter is related to Germany's future destiny. Hitler continued, "The current government is very willing to maintain friendly and beneficial relations with Soviet Russia, but the current government will curb the development of German communism to avoid shaking the entire Europe." Then Hitler submitted a bill authorizing the government, which granted the National Socialist Party unconditional full power within four years of its ruling period. During this period, the government has the right to enact laws that conflict with the constitution. The bill was immediately passed in Parliament with 441 votes against 94 votes. The minority votes contained the votes of the Social Democratic Party. After the vote, Parliament adjourned indefinitely.

Havas, Berlin, 23rd - The draft law granting the government full powers was recently passed by the House of Representatives with 441 votes against 94 votes. In front of the Kroll Opera House (the meeting place of the House of Representatives), there was a sea of people, including thousands of members of the National Socialist Party's military. Upon hearing the news of the passage of the bill, they cheered enthusiastically. Chancellor Hitler stood on the balcony and gave a brief speech to the people, saying that the first part of the National Socialist government's program has now been achieved, and the people should be loyal to the government so that it can complete its second plan. This plan is to give the German people freedom, honor, and power. After the passage of this full-power law, it is tantamount to granting dictatorial power to the government. All parties except the Socialist Party voted in favor of the bill.

Regarding the Northeast Provinces Issue

China and Japan Will Fight a Protracted War

Victory Will Ultimately Belong to China

丨An Observation by an American Missionary丨

(New York) Missionary Stanley Jones, who has lived in China and Japan for 23 years, recently issued a statement on the Manchurian issue, saying, "China and Japan will inevitably wage a series of wars over the Manchurian issue, and victory will ultimately belong to China. If we look at examples in world history, Manchuria is the 'Alsace-Lorraine' of the Far East." (Havas dispatch on the 23rd)

Germany Mistreats Jews

Ten Thousand American Jewish Veterans

Submit a Petition to the Mayor of New York

Reuter's, New York, 23rd - Ten thousand Jewish veterans marched to City Hall today and submitted a petition to Mayor O'Brien, protesting the German mistreatment of Jews in the country and suggesting a boycott of German goods.

Reuter's, Berlin, 23rd - Many people in Berlin laugh at the suggestions made by Americans that an economic boycott be put on Germany, as Germany always has a trade surplus with the United States. Political circles today admit that at the beginning of the national revolution, there were indeed acts of terror, but they have almost completely stopped today. The German government is now able to control everything. Speaker of the Reichstag Göring today accused the Social Democratic Party of spreading rumors abroad. If foreign Social Democratic newspapers continue to publish lies about Germany, the Social Democratic Party will suffer. Göring denied that German Jewish cemeteries had been excavated and said that he was willing to lead any foreign committee to visit the prisons to see if the prisoners were being tortured. It is reported that the German government plans to protest to the governments of various countries regarding the publication of such false news in their newspapers and plans to ban the import of such newspapers into Germany, paying particular attention to American newspapers.

Matsuoka Attempts to Lobby in the United States

(Tokyo) According to Japanese Foreign Ministry sources, Matsuoka Yosuke arrived safely in New York on the morning of the 22nd. Fearing assassination, he telegraphed the US government to send police to protect him before landing. He is said to be staying in New York for a few days before going to Washington. (Associated Press dispatch)

British Prime Minister Reports to Parliament

The Process of Negotiating the Four-Power Pact

Argues That Existing Treaties Need to be Revised

Reuter's, London, 23rd - British Prime Minister MacDonald today made a highly anticipated statement in the House of Commons, describing his visits to Geneva, Rome, and Paris. The Prime Minister said that when he and Foreign Secretary Simon arrived in Geneva,

Disarmament Was on the Verge of Collapse - They felt that the Disarmament Conference was in danger of collapsing, as the parties disagreed on the details and no work could be done.

Recognized Germany's Equality - They were forced to concede equality to Germany. Today is no longer a time when the great powers can use their combined strength to force any European nation to submit to obligations that they believe are contrary to their honor. He and Foreign Secretary Simon knew that what had to be made clear now was that the obligations imposed on any European country were honorable and responsible, and, more importantly, that these obligations were voluntarily assumed. However, recent events have greatly increased the dangers of proceeding in this way. Therefore, the British plan advocates that equality itself cannot be implemented during the transition period, but only seeks to end rearmament. Europe is now very uneasy and in a state of great anxiety, but the Disarmament Conference has been revitalized due to the intervention of him and Foreign Secretary Simon. The Prime Minister then spoke about his visit to Rome, saying that after arriving in Rome, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini showed him a short document.

Launched Four-Power Cooperation - It proposes to launch a four-power cooperation in Europe to maintain peace in the spirit of the Kellogg-Briand Pact and to recognize Germany's equal status in principle. The Italian plan proposes that the four powers agree not to use force to resolve any current political difficulties and proposes to immediately revise the treaty in accordance with Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant.

The Pact is Valid for Ten Years - If such a plan can become a pact, then the period of validity of this pact is ten years. The British government will now formulate detailed rules so that the Italian plan should be aimed solely at revising the treaty, rather than a general aim of peace. When a member of Parliament asked about the meaning of "revising the treaty and a general aim of peace," the Prime Minister replied that he meant that this plan not only has a general aim of peace, but must have a peaceful organization as its main and only aim.

Does Not Want to Exclude Small Countries - This plan must not exclude the participation of small countries, because small countries have a greater relationship in some respects than large countries, in order to eliminate the causes of conflict arising from existing treaties. The Prime Minister concluded by saying that when the inevitable revival of nationalism causes the peace treaties to be reopened for discussion, this kind of plan can prevent danger in Europe. The government then issued an official statement regarding the Prime Minister's statement that revising the treaty and having a general aim of peace, saying that the Prime Minister stated that the British government will deliberate on the details of this plan, so that this plan may not only have peace as a general aim, but also may not only take revising the treaty as a big and almost only detail.

Havas, London, 23rd - Prime Minister MacDonald gave a report on the diplomatic situation in the House of Commons. The meeting place was packed, and many diplomatic representatives from various countries were also present. From Prime Minister MacDonald's speech, it can be seen that the purpose of the British and Italian authorities is to revise the existing treaties, but the procedures for immediate implementation have not yet been determined. MacDonald said that the issue of German armaments has long been a cause of chaos, and all the current difficulties in Europe arise from this. If Europe wants to adopt a policy that can last, it must grant Germany equal rights in armaments. MacDonald used a concise document to explain the Italian Prime Minister Mussolini's plan, but he did not mention the details of its implementation. Its main spirit is that Germany agrees to cooperate with Britain, France, and Italy, and the three countries guarantee to make concessions to Germany on the principle of equal armaments in exchange. MacDonald argued that the existing treaties need to be revised based on Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant. If the four countries can cooperate within the scope of the League of Nations, then Britain will consider the methods of implementing the Italian Prime Minister's plan, the only important thing being the method of revising the treaty. However, MacDonald assured the Conservative Party that revising the treaty would not involve British colonies, and that if there were any actions against small countries, their opinions would be sought first. No changes will be made lightly until the countries have expressed their opinions.

(Note: Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant stipulates that the General Assembly may at any time request members of the League to review treaties that are no longer applicable and to consider international situations that may endanger world peace.)

The Issue of Arms Embargo and Disarmament

Questions in the British House of Commons

Reuter's, London, 23rd - Undersecretary of State for Foreign Affairs Captain Eden stated in the House of Commons today regarding the suggestion to ban the transport of arms to the Far East that it is impossible to agree on international action in a short period of time. Many countries must acquire powers that they do not have today. Judging from the experiences that Britain has gained in the past few weeks, if one wishes to take such effective action in the future, one must first establish the institutions for this action. When members of Parliament asked whether the negotiations in Geneva were based on the principle of simply banning the transport of arms to aggressor countries, Eden replied that as far as Britain is concerned, it is to study the issue of arms shipments to the Far East. This issue must be studied and decided internationally before it can be effective. One country cannot tell other countries how to act. Eden then spoke about the general issue of disarmament, saying that as a result of the suggestions made in Rome, small countries also have the opportunity to participate. This plan will be managed within the structure of the League of Nations in the future. Britain's disarmament plan encompasses various suggestions and has the best chance of being accepted by the sixty countries attending the Disarmament Conference. If the Disarmament Conference is willing to accept a slightly lower standard than that set in the plan, Britain has no objection. In short, if the representatives of the countries sign a draft treaty like today's, then a large part of disarmament can be achieved, and the conference can avoid failure. There is a great hope that the international community will accept this, which is a good sign. He is optimistic because the countries attending the Disarmament Conference now have to choose one of the British plan or a similar plan, otherwise they must endure the consequences of the conference's failure.

Novel

Fleeting Time in Dreams (11)

— Qin Shouou

"What's your name?" After letting her sit down on the sofa opposite him, Wu Yi initially wanted to read the newspaper by himself and ignore her. However, he could not resist this girl, who kept her clear, star-like eyes fixed on him, seemingly wanting to speak. Wu Yi had no choice but to start a conversation with her by asking her name.

"My surname is Mai, ... Mai E is my name!" An extremely direct and straightforward reply.

"Ah! An actress!" Wu Yi was secretly surprised, "Unexpectedly, an actress is so generous and quiet, ... and so beautiful ...!"

"So you are Boss Mai. I've heard of you for a long time!" He looked at this famous actress with an admiring and pleasant gaze, and formally started chatting with her; at the same time, he inevitably revealed his own name.

Mai E is a woman who has received secondary education and has a high level of knowledge. Although she is an actress, her daily actions are truly enough to shame ordinary female students who use books as decorations. She speaks very profoundly, and every word is worth savoring. Sometimes she can make people embarrassed to death, and sometimes she can make people laugh to tears. All of this, in the two hours of conversation at the Da Wang Chang Sheng Company, Wu Yi clearly recognized. From that day on, he realized that not all women are vulgar, not all women are shallow. In addition to the ordinary vulgar women, there is such an extraordinary flower, so he began to develop a kind of admiration and attachment for an extremely unusual woman that did not go beyond the scope of friendship.

Originally, Lin Daping would go to Mai E's house every night. Since Wu Yi got to know Mai E, he would often invite Wu Yi to go with him. After Wu Yi went with him a few times, his legs seemed to have a machine installed, and every time it was 5 o'clock, he would involuntarily follow Lin Daping smoothly to Mai E's house. Later, he gradually felt that if he wanted to be a person, a happy person, his daily schedule could not be missing a few hours of talking and laughing with Mai E.

However, Wu Yi is a newspaper reporter, and Mai E is an actress. Their working hours are both at night, and they both need to rest during the day. Therefore, Wu Yi gradually felt that going to Mai's house with Lin Daping for an hour or two after 5 o'clock every day was too cramped and inconvenient. One day, the bravest day, he boldly went to Mai E's house alone after the clock struck two, when Lin Daping was at the Tai Wang Company.

"Eh! ... You ..." When Wu Yi arrived at Mai's house, it happened that Mai E had just gotten up. Her oval face had no powder on it, as white as the sky after a rain. Her natural feet, without socks, were in a pair of embroidered slippers; she was wearing a pink bathrobe; her long, black hair was draped over her shoulders, standing in the intoxicating spring breeze, truly like a celestial maiden we see in our dreams.

When she saw Wu Yi, she greeted him with a shy and happy smile, and reached out her ivory-carved arms to help Wu Yi take off his coat.

"I came too early. Are you busy ...?" Wu Yi saw that the people in Mai E's house, and the supporting actors, all looked like they had just gotten up, and were busy running around in the various rooms. He felt uneasy, so he leaned against the edge of a square table and asked in an apologetic tone.

Movie Supplement

Hollywood is a Woman's World

— Xi Rong

People in America all say, "Hollywood actresses wear men's trousers." Although in reality, some actresses do like to wear men's trousers, such as Marlene Dietrich, who usually likes to wear men's clothing, as has already been introduced in this magazine. In addition, Mary Pickford also often wears men's trousers. However, this saying "wear men's trousers" (Woman stars "wear the pants"), does not refer to the literal meaning. Its meaning is that Hollywood women control men. To go a step further, it means that Hollywood is almost a woman's world.

Why is this? It can be seen from a very prominent and peculiar habit in Hollywood. What is this habit? It is that the husbands of female stars are often addressed by their wives' names. For example, even though it is clearly Douglas Fairbanks, people know it, but they insist on calling him "Mr. Crawford," because his wife is the famous Joan Crawford. Clearly the man is Frank Fay, but people insist on calling him "Mr. Stanwyck," which is the same reason. This does not indicate "the husband gains status through his wife," so the husband must follow the wife's surname, but just for fun, and it has become a common practice. As for the husbands of female stars, they dare not violate the teachings of humor and rise up in rebellion, so they can only pretend not to notice.

Therefore, Jack Oakie once said humorously, "They might as well reform the marriage ceremony in the future. From now on, men marry women, use the women's names, and live in the women's houses. Furthermore, women can marry men, divorce them, and then marry another man, and each time they marry a man, give him a number. For example, Miss Smith's third husband would be called 'Smith the Third.'" In this way, the title "Mr." can also be abolished. As for women, they are always Misses, and people always have to call them "Miss."

Women are always called "Miss" which is prevalent in Hollywood. Marie Dressler is over sixty years old, and people still call her Miss, and many people still think she is an old maid. In fact, she has been married, and her husband died a long time ago. Others such as the famous Bebe Daniels, Gloria Swanson, Janet Gaynor, Norma Shearer, etc., all have husbands, but no one calls them Mrs. Even Mary Pickford's husband, Douglas Fairbanks, who is very famous, has not been able to erase Pickford's name and be called Mrs. Fairbanks. In Hollywood, the title "Mrs." is fundamentally uncommon. This is also almost the trend in Shanghai. Many social butterflies, clearly having husbands at home, refuse to say their husbands' surnames outside, and insist on calling themselves Miss, which leads to many jokes and many men being fooled.

Movie Review

Review of "The Man Who Played God"

— Ling He

(The Man Who Played God)

Skillful Direction, Excellent Performance

The Whole Film is Full of the Beauty of Stillness

This is a rare masterpiece.

A middle-aged musician from a luxurious background is very popular with women because of his superb performance skills. Among them, a widow and a young girl are closest to him, and the young girl even proposes to him. The musician refuses her because of the age difference. Soon after, a violent loud noise deafens the musician's eardrums. He is discouraged and wants to commit suicide. Later, he feels the suffering of the world and does not hesitate to sacrifice himself to love others, so-called "setting his mind to do good." And he sends the young girl to her beloved. He gets along well with the widow with whom he once had an affair.

Of course, we do not praise such an idealistic story. However, under the current social structure, the general art-for-art people can comfort themselves by deceptively regarding art as a transcendental and supreme thing, and even using art as a tool for preaching. Thus, this musician should perish with his music, or at least "rebirth" himself in the "salvation" of his conscience. Then they should "donate" to others, and then they "do good" with their unused money.

However, although their intentions are despicable, the structure of the story is ingenious, extraordinary, unique, and not clichéd. Although the development of the plot is very simple, the whole film focuses on the evolution of the plot. Since this is the case, the director and the actors of this film are very strenuous.

First, let's talk about the director: he used a very simple and clear introduction to the whole play at the beginning, and later he used extremely long shots to enable the protagonist to perform very vividly in the most subtle actions. He gave all the supporting actors full play without hindering the important performances, and it was not confusing at all. For example, using a telescope to make the whole play progress step by step is a very clever technique. In short, he enables the play to grow and flourish completely in the "quiet" air, the whole is the beauty of "stillness", filled with silence. This has a very similar mood to "The Woman Disputed". Of course, this is a very difficult job, and it must have sufficient cultivation.

As for the performance of the protagonist George Arliss, it is really profound. We can see from his performance that he has a full understanding of the play. He completely grasped the characteristics of the so-called neurotic artist and understood them in detail. He is passionate, aloof, crazy, and disillusioned, and even in the most ordinary actions, he pours all his energy into it. It can be said that the whole play is his one-man show, how strenuous! But precisely because of this, he can give full play. Ah! In this film, we must admit that he is an outstanding performer, and he and John Barrymore, James Cagney, etc. can be called outstanding talents in the film industry.

Among the supporting actors, we admit that Ivan Simpson, who plays Battle, also performed very well.

Other aspects such as sound recording, set design, lighting, and dialogue are all appropriate and wonderful.

"Pursuit" and

"Morning in the City"

— Yan Nan

Both National Films Are Good

On the huge advertisements, we can find "Pursuit" from Xinguang, and "Morning in the City" from Beijing, which are released at the same time. Of course, the styles and meanings of these two films are very different, but on different paths, they each have their own strengths and have considerable success.

We already know that "Pursuit" is Tianyi Company's sound film. Li Minghui, who was famous for a while, spoke for the first time. It is a five-cornered complicated love drama. Of course, in this kind of allocation, only two people can succeed. A and B got married, and D and E also achieved their goals, only C was alone and lonely. But he is a silly boy, he should fail, he is not qualified to have a wrong love in the first place. Those two people, B and D, are really painful, because their marriages are very far-fetched, and they are prisoners of money marriages. However, the abnormality of society is exactly like this. The idea that "love" is for the purpose of "cohabitation" is indeed a bit too biased by the screenwriter. But in the modern Chinese environment, besides marriage, there is really no way to describe the success or failure of love. This film very thoroughly explains the phenomenon of so-called "free love", and arranged marriages are just about the same, which can really make many people wake up.

As for the director. I don't want to say anything. For all aspects of technology. I think it's very ordinary. The photography and editing. Are still good. Then, apart from the good plot. It is the performance. Ge Qingrong's work is very light. I think he is not very suitable. What Li Minghui did in the past. Most of them are lively little sisters. And this time, she is a capable and aggressive woman. A kind of arrogant and frivolous attitude, describing modern women, is penetrating. The Mandarin and the performance are very good. Although she is very suitable for the character's personality, I still think it's a bit too much. Ma Louqian. Is more than sufficient in combat, but lacks depth. Hu Xian's work is too little, which is a pity. The male Ma Dongwu, a capitalist with a "childlike heart", is very good. Using humorous actions to satirize the world, is ridiculous and hateful. Zhang Zhenduo is the best of the male roles.

Let's talk about "Morning in the City." It and "City Nights" have the same tune but different performances. But it is not as powerful as "City Nights". In its plot, we find that the understanding of society is indeed more than "Pursuit". Of course, the director deserves credit. If you don't mind asking for perfection, then there are not a few far-fetched places in the overall organization of the play. The set design is very good. The contrast of classes also adds to the material. The photography is better than "Pursuit". Of course, silent films are much easier than sound films in terms of the movement and position of the camera. In terms of editing. Very thoughtful. The fall of a man is still described with a dance hall, which is a bit too vulgar.

As for the actors. The three who are more important 丨 Wang Renmei, Gao Zhanfei, and Biao Congmei 丨 were replaced by others in the first three episodes. These three little actors are all good. Lu Shaohui is very promising. Tang Huaiqiu and Wang Guilin, suffer a little in makeup. The performances are all above the average level.

Movie Novel

Red Dust (VI)

— Jie Ke

"You 丨丨 Won't you go away?" she sobbed, pleading.

But Nice sneered, "I have something to do. Do you want me to guard him to the death?"

The woman trembled with anger. She raised her hand and slapped him hard. But Nice looked at her in surprise. Slowly, his eyes showed a kind of genuine interest.

"Very good," he said slowly and gently. "This may relieve you of some sorrow."

But Nice returned to the village at dusk, still thinking about Babelei. A tiger was roaring in the jungle again. Babelei rushed out of her room into the living room.

"What is that?" she asked tremblingly.

"That's a tiger," But Nice said with a relaxed smile. "He won't break in."

"Oh 丨丨" Babelei was relieved, she was about to return to her room, but But Nice walked in front of her.

"I'm sorry about this morning. Let me apologize 丨丨" he began to say.

"There's no need for that," the woman said calmly. "You just need to heal Geli. He's sleeping now." Babelei was about to close the door, but But Nice stopped her.

"Are we friends now?" he asked in a low voice.

"What does it matter?" The door closed in his face. He turned around and sat down at the table with Mike and Ju Tong, who looked at him strangely. "Luckily, Dan is gone," Mike said. Before he finished speaking, a sharp voice struck their eardrums out of thin air.

"Xi! Aren't you babies asleep yet?"

The three hurried to the corridor, the light from the window shone on Dan's muddy body, one hand holding a parrot, the other holding a hat. Behind her came a boatman, holding a flashlight and a gun. Two natives followed with Dan's luggage.

"What's wrong?" But Nice immediately asked.

"It's a long story! I'll tell you slowly later," Dan said, extremely tired.

"Don't make noise, do you know? A lady and her man are in the next room 丨丨 he is a patient," But Nice gently warned.

"Oh 丨丨 I didn't know," the woman's voice was concerned. "Can I help?"

The next morning, she was sitting eating breakfast, Babelei walked into the living room, and suddenly saw another woman, and stopped in surprise.

"Hey, hello," Dan called cordially.

"Good morning," Babelei answered absentmindedly. "I am Mrs. Welles."

"I know," Dan replied. "They told me your husband is sick. Is he better today?"

"I don't know," the other woman said suspiciously. "Whose wife is here?"

"No. I'm Dan Zhan Huachen 丨丨 from Virginia," Dan explained proudly.
